<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:красть.html>красть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krastʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<ol><li>to sneak <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">somewhere</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>

***прокричать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прокричать.html>прокрича́ть</a> (7079)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кричать.html>крича́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kričátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прокричать.html>прокрича́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prokričátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to shout, to cry out, to yell
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прокричать.html>прокрича́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́ши</a> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> чём-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prokričátʹ</b> úši komú-libo o čóm-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to din something into someone's ears</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to shout <i>(for a certain time)</i>, to scream
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:прокричать.html>прокрича́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:целый.html>це́лый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>час</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oná <b>prokričála</b> célyj čas</i> ― <span class="e-translation">she screamed for a whole hour</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to trumpet, to tout
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прокричать.html>прокрича́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:успех.html>успе́хах</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prokričátʹ</b> ob uspéxax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to trumpet one's success</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прокрутить.html>прокрути́вший</a> (23714)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***прокрутить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прокрутить.html>прокрути́ть</a> (23714)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крутить.html>крути́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krutítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прокрутить.html>прокрути́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prokrutítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прокручивать.html>прокру́чивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to turn over</li>
<li>to play back, to replay
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прокрутить.html>прокрути́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пленка.html>плёнку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prokrutítʹ</b> pljónku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to play back the tape</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прокрутить.html>прокрути́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:память.html>па́мяти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:происшествие.html>происше́ствие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prokrutítʹ</b> v pámjati proisšéstvije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to reproduce/replay the incident in one's memory/mind</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to scroll
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прокрутить.html>прокрути́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вниз.html>вниз</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prokrutítʹ</b> vniz</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to scroll down</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прокручивать.html>прокру́чивать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вверх.html>вверх</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prokrúčivatʹ vverx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">scroll up</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to put across, to put through</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get turned over, to make a quick gain</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прокру́тка</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prokrútka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***прокручивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прокручивать.html>прокру́чивать</a> (24253)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прокрутить.html>прокрути́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prokrutítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прокручивать.html>прокру́чивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prokrúčivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прокрутить.html>прокрути́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to turn over</li>
<li>to play back, to replay
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прокручивать.html>прокру́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пленка.html>плёнку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prokrúčivatʹ</b> pljónku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to play back the tape</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прокручивать.html>прокру́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:память.html>па́мяти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:происшествие.html>происше́ствие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prokrúčivatʹ</b> v pámjati proisšéstvije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to reproduce/replay the incident in one's memory/mind</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to scroll
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прокручивать.html>прокру́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вниз.html>вниз</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prokrúčivatʹ</b> vniz</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to scroll down</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прокручивать.html>прокру́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вверх.html>вверх</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prokrúčivatʹ</b> vverx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">scroll up</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to put across, to put through</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get turned over, to make a quick gain</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прокру́тка</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prokrútka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***прокурить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прокурить.html>прокури́ть</a> (13479)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курить.html>кури́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kurítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прокурить.html>прокури́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prokurítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">проку́ривать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fill with tobacco smoke, to smoke up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прокурить.html>прокури́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:комната.html>ко́мнату</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prokuríli</b> vsju kómnatu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">they have smoked up the whole room</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spend on smoking</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***пролегать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пролегать.html>пролега́ть</a> (20506)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">проле́г-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prolég-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пролегать.html>пролега́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prolegátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пролечь.html>проле́чь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lie, to run
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>дорога</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пролегать.html>пролега́ла</a></b>/<a href = vnd.unilang:пролечь.html>пролегла́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:через.html>че́рез</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пол.html>по́ле</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">doroga <b>prolegála</b>/proleglá čerez pole</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the path lay/ran across a field</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:между.html>ме́жду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>ни́ми</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пролегать.html>пролега́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пропасть.html>пропасть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">méždu ními <b>prolegájet</b> propastʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">there is a chasm between them</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***пролежать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пролежать.html>пролежа́ть</a> (9688)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лежать.html>лежа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ležátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пролежать.html>пролежа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proležátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пролёживать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lie <i>(for a certain time)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>весь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пролежать.html>пролежа́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on vesʹ denʹ <b>proležál</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he spent the whole day lying down; he spent the whole day (lying) in bed</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to remain <i>(for a certain time)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посылка.html>посы́лка</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пролежать.html>пролежа́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>две</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неделя.html>неде́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:почта.html>по́чте</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">posýlka <b>proležála</b> dve nedéli na póčte</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the parcel lay for two weeks in the post office</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to get a bedsore <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пролежать.html>пролежа́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:спина.html>спи́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>proležál</b> spínu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he has a bedsore on his back; his back has gone numb</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cause to sink/sag down <i>(by lying on it)</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***пролезать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пролезать.html>пролеза́ть</a> (21708)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пролезть.html>проле́зть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proléztʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пролезать.html>пролеза́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prolezátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пролезть.html>проле́зть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get through, to wriggle through, to climb through, to squeeze through</li>
<li>to go <i>(through)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шкаф.html>шкаф</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пролезать.html>пролеза́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>дверь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">škaf ne <b>prolezájet</b> v dverʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the wardrobe won't go through the door</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to worm oneself <i>(into)</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пролезть.html>проле́зть</a> (9790)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лезть.html>лезть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">leztʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пролезть.html>проле́зть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proléztʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пролезать.html>пролеза́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get through, to wriggle through, to climb through, to squeeze through</li>
<li>to go <i>(through)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шкаф.html>шкаф</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пролезть.html>проле́зет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>дверь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">škaf ne <b>prolézet</b> v dverʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the wardrobe won't go through the door</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to worm oneself <i>(into)</i></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пролетарий.html>пролета́рий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proletárij</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пролетарий.html>пролета́рия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пролетарий.html>пролета́рии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пролетарий.html>пролета́риев</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пролетарский.html>пролета́рский</a></b>)

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пролетарий.html>пролета́рии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всех</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:страна.html>стра́н</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:соединяться.html>соединя́йтесь</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Proletárii vsex stran, sojedinjájtesʹ!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Workers of the world, unite!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***пролетать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пролетать.html>пролета́ть</a> (7892)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летать.html>лета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пролетать.html>пролета́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proletátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пролететь.html>пролете́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fly <i>(by, past, through)</i>, to fly <i>(over)</i></li>
<li>to overfly, to overshoot
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пролетать.html>пролета́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мимо.html>ми́мо</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цель.html>це́ли</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>proletátʹ</b> mímo céli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to overshoot the target</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cover, to pass rapidly</li>
<li><i>(time)</i> to fly by</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be passed over <i>(for)</i>, to miss the mark, to miss the boat
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пролетать.html>пролета́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:фанера.html>фане́ра</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> пари́жем</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">proletátʹ kak fanéra nad Parížem</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">miss the mark, miss the boat</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">to fly like plywood over Paris</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***пролететь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пролететь.html>пролете́ть</a> (5453)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лететь.html>лете́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пролететь.html>пролете́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proletétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пролетать.html>пролета́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fly <i>(by, past, through)</i>, to fly <i>(over)</i></li>
<li>to overfly, to overshoot
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>мы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пролететь.html>пролете́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:знак.html>знак</a> "<a href = vnd.unilang:стоп.html>стоп</a>"</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">my <b>proletéli</b> znak "stop"</i> ― <span class="e-translation">we overshot the [stop] sign</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cover, to pass rapidly</li>
<li><i>(time)</i> to fly by
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пролететь.html>пролете́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>две</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неделя.html>неде́ли</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>proletéli</b> dve nedéli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">two weeks flew by</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be passed over <i>(for)</i>, to miss the mark, to miss the boat
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пролететь.html>пролете́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:повышение.html>повыше́нием</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>proletél</b> s povyšénijem</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he was passed over for</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пролить.html>проли́в</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prolív</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пролив.html>проли́ва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пролив.html>проли́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пролив.html>проли́вов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>strait, channel
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пролить.html>проли́в</a></b> па-де-кале́</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prolív</b> Pa-de-Kalé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Strait of Dover</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пролить.html>проли́в</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:золотой.html>золоты́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ворот.html>воро́та</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prolív</b> Zolotýje Voróta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Golden Gate strait</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
